pool.dataset.create
===================

Creates a dataset/zvol.

.. examples(websocket)::

  Create a dataset within tank pool.

    :::javascript {
        "id": "6841f242-840a-11e6-a437-00e04d680384", "msg": "method", "method": "pool.dataset.create, "params": [{ "name": "tank/myuser", "comments": "Dataset for myuser" }] }
